### [1] [Noise2Params: Unification and Parameter Determination from Noise via a Probabilistic Event Camera Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16317)
*Owen Root,Julinda Mujo,Min Xu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出基于光子统计的统一概率模型，贯通事件相机静态噪声与S曲线；给出三种强度区间下的分布近似，并据此提出仅用静态均匀场即可估计相机关键参数的Noise2Params方法；用合成噪声训练CNN并在实测上验证与提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 事件相机缺乏精确统一的成因模型，导致标定困难、算法与噪声处理割裂。现有对S曲线与静态噪声的解释彼此分离，且标定常需复杂动态光源，实验门槛高。

Method: 从光子到达的泊松统计出发，推导事件触发概率的统一模型，覆盖所有光强：精确泊松、鞍点近似、高斯近似三种表述，统一解释静态噪声与S曲线并揭示阈值选择的细微性。在此基础上提出Noise2Params：通过拟合静态均匀场下观测到的噪声事件分布，最小化误差以估计对数对比度阈值B、流明到光子转换系数α、以及强度相关的泄漏项θ。进一步用该分布合成噪声图像训练CNN，并在实验静态场景重建任务上评估；比较仅用实测数据训练与加入合成数据的差异。

Result: 统一模型成功再现实验中的静态噪声统计与S曲线形态，并指出S曲线并非简单固定阈值。Noise2Params在无需动态光源的条件下稳健估计B、α、θ（θ呈强度依赖）。用模型生成的合成噪声训练的CNN能从实测数据中更好地重建静态场景；结合合成数据的模型优于仅用实测数据训练。

Conclusion: 提出的概率统一框架为事件相机提供了定量化基础，可简化校准流程、提升噪声感知算法设计，并在光子受限条件下具备应用价值；合成数据与实测数据的结合进一步改善了学习型方法性能。

Abstract: Accurate, unified models for event cameras (ECs) remain elusive, hampering calibration and algorithm design. We develop a foundational probabilistic model for EC event detection, grounded in photon statistics, that unifies the description of static scene noise events and step response curves (S-curves) within a single analytical framework. Three formulations of the probability distributions are derived, spanning all intensity regimes: exact Poisson, saddle-point, and Gaussian. The model reveals the underlying connection between these otherwise disparate EC behaviors and clarifies the interpretation of S-curves, which we show is more nuanced than selecting a fixed probability threshold. Based on this model, we propose Noise2Params, a method for determining camera-specific values of the log-contrast threshold $B$, the lux-to-photon conversion factor $α$, and the leakage term $θ$ (found to be intensity dependent), via error minimization against observed noise-event distributions. Noise2Params requires only recordings of static, uniform scenes, offering an experimentally accessible alternative to approaches that demand specialized dynamic light sources. We further support the validity the model by training convolutional neural networks (CNNs) on synthetic noise images generated from our distributions and evaluating their ability to reconstruct static scenes from experimental data. We further demonstrate the utility of our model by showing that CNNs incorporating synthetic data outperform those trained solely on experimental data. Our framework provides a quantitative foundation for EC calibration, noise-aware algorithm design, and applications in photon-limited regimes.

</details>


### [2] [StrLoRA: Towards Streaming Continual Visual Instruction Tuning for MLLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16353)
*Chang Che,Ziqi Wang,Hui Ma,Cheems Wang,Zenglin Shi*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出Streaming CVIT (StrCVIT)设定与方法StrLoRA，在连续、混合任务的数据流中进行多模态指令微调，显著缓解遗忘并提升能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有持续视觉指令微调多在任务增量（每阶段单一预定义任务）设定下研究，难以反映真实世界中任务交织、动态演化的连续数据流；模型需要同时学习新能力、巩固旧能力并避免遗忘，现有方法在混合任务块内难以区分与适配异构样本。

Method: 提出更通用的StrCVIT设定与两阶段专家路由框架StrLoRA：1) 阶段一基于文本指令进行任务感知的稀疏专家选择，激活与当前指令相关的一小部分专家以减少跨任务干扰；2) 阶段二在所选专家内进行token级专家加权，利用局部视觉token与全局指令表示的跨模态注意力计算贡献权重；并加入路由稳定性正则，用EMA历史路由分布作为参考对齐，以适应非平稳数据流。

Result: 在新构建的StrCVIT基准上，StrLoRA显著优于现有CVIT方法，在连续演化数据流中更好地提升模型能力并缓解遗忘。

Conclusion: StrCVIT更贴近真实流式场景；StrLoRA通过任务感知稀疏路由、token级跨模态加权与稳定性正则，实现对混合任务流的有效适配与稳健学习。

Abstract: Continual Visual Instruction Tuning (CVIT) enables Multimodal Large Language Models to incrementally acquire new abilities. However, existing CVIT methods operate under a restrictive task-incremental setting, where each training phase corresponds to a single, predefined task. This does not reflect real-world conditions, where data arrives as a continuous stream of interleaved and dynamically evolving tasks. To bridge this gap, we introduce Streaming CVIT (StrCVIT), a more general and realistic setting where models learn from a stream of data chunks containing a dynamic mixture of tasks. In StrCVIT, a model must simultaneously acquire new abilities, reinforce recurring abilities, and mitigate forgetting. Existing CVIT methods fail here as they cannot reliably distinguish or adapt to the heterogeneous task samples within each chunk. We therefore propose StrLoRA, a regularized two-stage expert routing framework. StrLoRA first performs task-aware expert selection using the textual instruction to activate a sparse subset of relevant experts, reducing cross-task interference. It then applies token-wise expert weighting within this subset, where contribution weights are computed via cross-modal attention between local visual tokens and the global instruction representation. To maintain stability across the non-stationary stream, a routing-stability regularization aligns current routing distributions with a historical exponential moving average reference. Extensive experiments on a newly developed StrCVIT benchmark show that StrLoRA substantially outperforms existing methods, effectively enhancing model's abilities from continuously evolving data streams.

</details>


### [3] [How Many Visual Tokens Do Multimodal Language Models Need? Scaling Visual Token Pruning with F^3A](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16359)
*YiJie Huang,Yiqun Zhang,Zhuoyue Jia,Xiaocui Yang,Junzhao Huang,Zihan Wang,Shi Feng,Daling Wang,Yifei Zhang,Yongkang Liu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出F^3A：一种在LLM读取图像token前进行、免训练的视觉token路由/裁剪方法，以固定预算下按任务检索证据，显著降低视觉token且保持性能与推理流程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有多模态模型通过增加视觉token提升感知，但推理成本高；训练免裁剪方法多依赖一次性代理指标（注意力、相似度、多样性），在高压缩与不同模型规模下不稳健。作者将问题重释为“任务条件的证据搜索”，以在固定预算下更有效分配视觉token。

Method: 提出F^3A——一个免训练、前置的视觉token路由器：1) 构建与问题相关的轻量提示线索；2) 通过冻结的稀疏感知头将线索与视觉网格token匹配；3) 用粗到细的证据定位与局部细化选择token；4) 通过覆盖保持的竞争机制分配预算；5) 对覆盖不足区域进行恢复；无需额外LLM前向、无需改动多模态提示与解码流程。

Result: 在固定视觉token预算下，F^3A可在激进压缩场景中优于基于注意力/相似度/多样性的一次性裁剪方法，跨模型规模保持鲁棒，同时不增加训练或额外LLM推理成本。（具体指标未在摘要给出）

Conclusion: 将视觉token裁剪视为任务条件证据搜索更合理；F^3A在无需训练和不改变原有推理管线的前提下，高效路由并分配有限视觉token，降低推理成本且维持或提升性能。

Abstract: Vision-language models improve perception by feeding increasingly long visual token sequences into language backbones, but the resulting inference cost raises a basic scaling question: as multimodal models grow, how many visual tokens are actually needed, and how should they be allocated under a fixed visual token budget? Existing training-free pruning methods typically answer this with one-shot proxies such as decoder attention, visual similarity, or conditional diversity. We argue that visual token pruning is better viewed as task-conditioned evidence search, especially under aggressive compression and across model scales. We propose F^3A, a training-free router for visual token pruning that operates before the language model consumes image tokens. F^3A builds lightweight question-conditioned cues, matches them to visual-grid tokens through frozen sparse sensing heads, and allocates a fixed vision token budget via coarse evidence localization, local refinement, coverage-preserving competition, and recovery of under-covered regions. It requires no model training, no extra LLM forward pass and preserves the original multimodal prompting and decoding pipeline.

</details>


### [4] [Fre-Res: Frequency-Residual Video Token Compression for Efficient Video MLLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16366)
*Yigui Feng,Qinglin Wang,Yang Liu,Jie Liu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: Fre-Res提出一种预算自适应的双轨视频token压缩：保留稀疏高保真空间锚点，并用频域化的时间残差紧凑表征时序变化，在保证精度的同时显著减少视觉token长度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 视频多模态大模型在空间细节与时间覆盖间存在矛盾：细粒度视觉需要大量空间token，而捕捉短暂事件需密集时间采样，导致计算/上下文预算受限。需要一种既保留关键细节又高效覆盖时间的表示方式。

Method: 提出Fre-Res：1) 双轨设计：稀疏高保真空间锚点+致密时间演化的残差-频率token；2) 在视觉潜空间对帧间残差轨迹做1D-DCT，利用低频能量集中性实现紧凑编码；3) 空间引导吸收器（Spatial-Guided Absorber）将时间残差信息注入其空间对应的锚点，使频域动态与原生视觉嵌入对齐；4) 预算自适应地调节锚点数与频率分量数。

Result: 在短视频与长视频推理基准上，以更少的视觉token达到或逼近全token性能，实现更优的精度-效率权衡；消融显示：时间频域残差保留因果转移线索；空间锚点对细粒度目标与布局推理至关重要。

Conclusion: 将空间细节与时间动态解耦并以频域残差压缩时间信息，可在不显著牺牲性能下大幅缩短视频token长度；该范式为视频MLLM在有限上下文预算下的高效推理提供了通用思路。

Abstract: Video MLLMs face a persistent tension between spatial fidelity and temporal coverage: preserving fine-grained visual details requires many spatial tokens, while capturing short-lived events requires dense temporal sampling. We propose \textbf{Fre-Res}, a budget-adaptive dual-track video-token compression framework that separates these two forms of evidence. Fre-Res preserves sparse high-fidelity spatial anchors and represents dense temporal evolution through compact residual-frequency tokens. Specifically, it applies temporal 1D-DCT to inter-frame residual trajectories in vision-latent space, where we observe strong low-frequency concentration. To align frequency-domain dynamics with native visual embeddings, Fre-Res introduces a Spatial-Guided Absorber that injects temporal residual information into spatially corresponding anchor tokens. Across fine-grained short-video and long-video reasoning benchmarks, Fre-Res achieves a favorable accuracy--efficiency trade-off, matching or approaching full-token performance while substantially reducing visual-token length. Extensive ablations further show that temporal-frequency residuals preserve causal transition cues, while spatial anchors remain essential for fine-grained object and layout reasoning.

</details>


### [5] [GeoSym127K: Scalable Symbolically-verifiable Synthesis for Multimodal Geometric Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16371)
*Jinhao Jing,Zheng Ma,Jinwei Liang,Qiannian Zhao,Shawn Chen,Jing Yang,Por Lip Yee,Prayag Tiwari,Jingjing Bai,Benyou Wang,Lewei Lu,Zhan Su*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出GeoSym Engine神经-符号框架，生成精确几何符号真值与高质量图像，构建GeoSym127K与GeoSym-Bench，并通过SFT与RLVR显著提升LMM几何推理表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LMM在几何推理上受视觉幻觉与缺乏严格数学CoT数据限制，难以进行多步、图依赖的逻辑推理。需要可扩展、可验证的数据与训练范式来提升几何推理的精确性与稳健性。

Method: 提出GeoSym Engine：基于类型条件语法与解析型SymGT求解器生成精确的符号级标注，配合渲染管线得到高精度几何图。由此构建难度分层数据集GeoSym127K（51K图、127K问、含符号真值与55K经答案验证的CoT对），并发布专家策划评测集GeoSym-Bench（511题）。模型训练采用监督微调（SFT）以及基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR，GRPO），其中SFT提供结构化起点。

Result: 在图依赖、多步几何题上取得集中提升：Qwen3-VL-8B在MathVerse Vision-Only子集提升+22.21%，在WeMath达61.52%（+6.19%），超越如Doubao-1.8等闭源模型。RLVR从结构化SFT检查点出发优于零样本RL，表现上限显著提高。

Conclusion: 神经-符号可验证数据与训练范式能系统缓解长程逻辑碎片化，推动LMM几何推理可扩展提升；确定性的精确匹配奖励为可验证推理合成展示出良好扩展潜力。

Abstract: Large Multimodal Models (LMMs) often struggle with geometric reasoning due to visual hallucinations and a lack of mathematically precise Chain-of-Thought (CoT) data. To address this, we propose the GeoSym Engine, an automated and scalable neuro-symbolic framework. By leveraging a type-conditional grammar and an analytic SymGT Solver, it derives exact symbolic ground truths and seamlessly integrates with a robust rendering pipeline to produce high-precision geometric diagrams. Using this engine, we construct GeoSym127K, a difficulty-stratified dataset featuring 51K high-resolution images, 127K questions with symbolic ground truths, and 55K answer-verified CoT QA pairs. We also introduce GeoSym-Bench, an expert-curated suite of 511 complex samples for rigorous evaluation. Through extensive supervised fine-tuning (SFT), we demonstrate that GeoSym drives concentrated improvements specifically on diagram-dependent and multi-step geometry tasks. Our Qwen3-VL-8B model gains an absolute +22.21% on the MathVerse Vision-Only subset and reaches 61.52% (+6.19% improvement) on WeMath, mitigating long-horizon logic fragmentation and outperforming advanced closed-source models like Doubao-1.8. Furthermore, applying Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) via GRPO reveals that initializing from structural SFT checkpoints substantially elevates the performance ceiling over zero-shot RL. Driven by deterministic exact-match signals, this showcases the robust scaling potential of our verifiable reasoning synthesis. Datasets and code are available at https://huggingface.co/datasets/Tomie0506/GeoSym127K and https://github.com/Tomie56/GeoSym127K.

</details>


### [6] [SwordBench: Evaluating Orthogonality of Steering Image Representations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16372)
*Vladimir Zaigrajew,Dawid Pludowski,Hubert Baniecki,Przemyslaw Biecek*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出SwordBench，一个用于在视觉模型中进行概念引导/干预的基准，定义并评估跨概念鲁棒性与附带伤害，比较多种表示操控方法，发现线性SVM虽分离与正交性好但仍有非零附带伤害，稀疏自编码器在副作用上更优；在简单任务中也难以实现完美操控。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有关于推理时对模型表征进行引导/干预的评估主要局限在语言建模且任务含糊，缺乏在视觉领域、跨主干与多概念移除任务上的系统性与可复现实验框架。作者为了解决评估空缺，并更细粒度刻画正交化在实际引导中的二阶影响，提出新的度量与基准。

Method: 1) 构建SwordBench：覆盖多种视觉主干模型与多类概念移除/引导任务的统一测试套件；2) 定义两类新度量：跨概念鲁棒性（在对某概念做正交化时，其他概念的检测稳定性）与附带伤害（对不含偏置输入的下游性能影响）；3) 评测与比较多种表示操控方法，包括线性SVM、稀疏自编码器、标准基线与优化式方法；4) 分析概念激活向量正交化带来的二阶效应。

Result: 线性SVM在可分性与正交性上表现最佳，但无法实现零附带伤害，且常不如稀疏自编码器在副作用控制上；在较简单设置中，无论是标准基线还是优化式方法都未能实现“完美引导”（既去除目标概念又不影响无偏样本的任务性能）。

Conclusion: SwordBench为视觉模型表征引导提供统一评测与新度量，揭示正交化并非万灵药：更高分离度不必然意味着更低副作用。当前方法在实现无副作用、完美操控方面仍存在显著差距，提示未来需在鲁棒引导与副作用最小化上探索新方法。

Abstract: Steering or intervening on model representations at inference time to correct predictions is essential for AI interpretability and safety, yet existing evaluation protocols are limited to ambiguous language modeling tasks. To address this gap, we introduce SwordBench, a benchmark for steering image representations of vision models across multiple backbones and concept removal tasks. Beyond a unified benchmarking suite, we propose new evaluation notions that uncover the second-order effects of orthogonalization among concept activation vectors for pragmatic steering. Specifically, cross-concept robustness measures the stability of concept detection performance across inputs orthogonalized against alternative concepts, and collateral damage quantifies whether steering inadvertently affects model performance on a downstream task for inputs lacking the bias. We find that although a linear support vector machine exhibits superior separability and orthogonality, it fails to achieve zero collateral damage, often trailing sparse autoencoders. In simpler regimes, both standard baselines and optimization-based methods fail to achieve perfect steering. The source code will be made available soon on GitHub.

</details>


### [7] [Cross-Source Supervision for Bone Infection Segmentation in Dual-Modality PET-CT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16373)
*Zonglin Yang,Xiaolei Diao,Jishizhan Chen,Xiaozhuang Man,Wei Kong,Gen Wen,Pengfei Cheng,Daqian Shi*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出用于骨感染分割的PET-CT早期融合与双源解耦学习框架，并以患者级3D评估验证其在标注分歧下的稳健性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 骨感染的准确诊断与病灶定位对治疗关键；PET-CT兼具代谢与解剖信息，但病灶边界模糊、不同专家/系统标注不一致，导致分割困难与评估偏差，尤其小样本数据中二维评测易夸大性能。

Method: 1) 构建PET代谢与CT骨窗解剖的早期融合双模态端到端分割模型；2) 放弃传统2D切片级评估，采用患者级3D体素/体积评估与交叉验证以减少切片相关性引起的性能膨胀；3) 提出解耦的双源学习：并行训练两套模型，分别以高敏感度与高特异度的专家标注/临床意图为监督；4) 通过交叉评估矩阵量化两模型在不同标注/诊断哲学下的泛化与互补性。

Result: 在患者级别给出均值±标准差（以及均值−标准差）客观报告，显示PET-CT多模态融合优于单模态；交叉评估表明模型内化了不同专家的诊断取向（高敏与高特），在存在标注分歧时依然保持稳健表现与多样性。

Conclusion: 早期融合的PET-CT分割结合解耦双源学习与严格患者级3D评估，可在标注不一致场景下实现稳健、可解释且临床友好的骨感染分割，为保留诊断多样性的临床AI部署提供范式。

Abstract: Early and accurate diagnosis and lesion localization of bone infections are crucial for clinical treatment. PET-CT integrates anatomical information from CT with metabolic information from PET, making it an important imaging modality for diagnosing bone infections. However, accurate lesion segmentation remains challenging due to indistinct lesion boundaries and inconsistencies in annotations generated by different experts or automated systems. In this work, we investigate multimodal segmentation of bone infections under annotation discrepancy. We develop a bimodal end-to-end segmentation framework that integrates PET metabolic signals and CT bone-window anatomy through an early-fusion multimodal representation.To mitigate performance inflation caused by inter-slice correlation in small datasets, this study discards traditional two-dimensional evaluation methods and implements a rigorous patient-level 3D volumetric evaluation and cross-validation. Furthermore, instead of forcing a singular consensus, we propose a decoupled dual-source learning framework where parallel models are trained on independent expert annotations driven by high-sensitivity and high-specificity clinical intents. Experimental results objectively report performance variations at the patient level (Mean + SD and Mean - SD), demonstrating the effectiveness of multimodal PET-CT fusion. The cross-evaluation matrix quantitatively reveals how models successfully internalize distinct expert diagnostic philosophies, providing a robust, diversity-preserving paradigm for clinical AI deployment in bone infection segmentation.

</details>


### [8] [StreamPro: From Reactive Perception to Proactive Decision-Making in Streaming Video](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16381)
*Ao Li,Zihan Xiao,Zihao Yue,Boshen Xu,Linli Yao,Jiaze Li,Pei Fu,Jianzhong Ju,Jian Luan,Qin Jin*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出StreamPro-Bench评测与StreamPro训练框架，面向流式视频的前摄（主动）理解与决策；在不完整观察下优化“何时回答+答什么”，显著提升早判可靠性与实时表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准多为“看完再答”，只在显式证据出现后触发回答，无法评估在部分观测下的及时可靠决策能力；训练上，流式轨迹中“沉默”远多于“响应”，且需同时优化正确性与时机，导致监督极度不均衡与多目标难优化。

Method: 1) 基准：构建StreamPro-Bench，从三维度评测——感知理解、时间推理与主动能动性（在证据不全时的早而准决策）。2) 训练框架StreamPro：两阶段。阶段一SFT引入CB-Stream Loss缓解监督不均衡；阶段二采用GRPO（Group Relative Policy Optimization）并设计多粒度奖励，结合回合级与轨迹级信号共同优化“何时/如何答”。

Result: 在StreamPro-Bench上得分41.5，显著超过此前最佳10.4；在实时流式基准StreamingBench-RTVU上得分78.9，保持强劲实时性能。

Conclusion: 通过新基准与两阶段主动学习范式，模型能在不完全观测下做更早且更可靠的响应，实现前摄视频理解的性能跃迁，同时兼顾准确性与时机优化。

Abstract: Proactive streaming video understanding requires models to continuously process video streams and decide when to respond, rather than merely what to respond. This naturally introduces a decision-making problem under partial observations, where models must balance early prediction against sufficient evidence. However, existing benchmarks largely follow a "see-then-answer" paradigm, where responses are triggered only after explicit evidence appears, effectively reducing proactive reasoning to delayed perception. As a result, they fail to evaluate a model's ability to make timely and reliable decisions under incomplete observations. Moreover, training proactive models is inherently challenging due to the extreme imbalance between silence and response signals in streaming trajectories, as well as the need to jointly optimize response correctness and timing. To address these challenges, we introduce StreamPro-Bench, a new benchmark that evaluates streaming models from three complementary perspectives: Perception Understanding, Temporal Reasoning, and Proactive Agency, where the last measures a model's ability to make early yet reliable decisions under partial observations. We further propose StreamPro, a two-stage training framework for proactive learning. First, we introduce CB-Stream Loss to mitigate the severe supervision imbalance during supervised fine-tuning (SFT). Then, we apply Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) with a multi-grained reward design that involves both turn-level and trajectory-level rewards. Experiments show that StreamPro significantly improves proactive performance. On StreamPro-Bench, it achieves 41.5, substantially outperforming the previous best (10.4), while also maintaining strong performance on real-time streaming benchmarks, achieving 78.9 on StreamingBench-RTVU.

</details>


### [9] [A neurosymbolic Approach with Epistemic Deep Learning for Hierarchical Image Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16383)
*Ezel Kilicdere,Shireen Kudukkil Manchingal,Fabio Cuzzolin*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一个结合焦集推理与可微模糊逻辑的神经符号框架，增强Swin Transformer用于分层图像分类，既保持精度又提升不确定性校准与层级一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 深度网络在图像分类中常过度自信、难表达认识不确定性，且在分层分类中易违背粗细粒度之间的逻辑一致性；需要一种既能建模不确定性又能强制结构约束的方法。

Method: 在Swin Transformer上引入“焦集（focal sets）”以在嵌入空间中表示对多个细粒度类别的信念质量；构建信念理论层，使用模糊隶属函数与t-范数合取来将细粒度与粗粒度预测耦合，鼓励层级一致；设计可学习的损失以权衡校准、质量（mass）正则与逻辑一致性，实现数据证据与符号结构的自适应折中。

Result: 在分层图像分类实验中，与Transformer基线精度相当；但预测更校准、解释性更强，过度自信显著减少，层级输出的一致性更高。

Conclusion: 将焦集推理与可微模糊逻辑结合，为同时具备准确性与认识不确定性感知的深度模型提供了可行路径，尤其适用于需要层级一致性的任务。

Abstract: Deep neural networks achieve high accuracy on image classification tasks. Yet, they often produce overconfident predictions as which fail to express epistemic uncertainty, and frequently violate logical or structural constraints present in the data. These limitations are particularly pronounced in hierarchical classification, where predictions across fine and coarse levels must remain coherent. We propose, for the first time, a unified neurosymbolic and epistemic modelling framework that augments Swin Transformers with focal set reasoning and differentiable fuzzy logic. Rather than treating labels as isolated categories, our method induces data-driven focal sets within the learnt embedding space, which helps capture epistemic uncertainty over multiple plausible fine-grained classes. These focal sets form the basis of a belief-theoretic layer that uses fuzzy membership functions and t-norm conjunctions to encourage consistency between fine- and coarse-grained predictions. A learnable loss further balances calibration, mass regularisation, and logical consistency, allowing the model to adaptively trade off symbolic structure with data-driven evidence. In experiments on hierarchical image classification, our framework maintains accuracy on par with transformer baselines while providing more calibrated and interpretable predictions, reducing overconfidence and enforcing high logical consistency across hierarchical outputs. Our experimental results show that combining focal set reasoning with fuzzy logic provides a practical step toward deep learning models that are both accurate and epistemically aware.

### [10] [Mutual Enhancement Between Global Tokens and Patch Tokens: From Theory to Practice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16384)
*Xiusheng Huang,Xin Jiang,Jun Zhao,Kang Liu,Yequan Wang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: TaTok 提出一种基于信息熵的自适应图像离散化（tokenization）框架，通过全局token建模互信息与动态token过滤（DTF）按信息密度分配token，实现更高压缩率与更准重建，并带来更优gFID和显著推理加速。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有图像tokenization方法以固定压缩率对所有区域一刀切，忽视图像中信息密度的空间差异，导致在复杂区域信息丢失、在简单区域冗余过多，从而影响长序列建模效率与重建质量。作者希望引入信息论视角，兼顾压缩率、信息充分性与去冗余性。

Method: 1) 理论分析指出两大问题：仅用patch token重建存在信息不足；patch token之间存在显著冗余。2) 设计全局token来显式建模patch之间的互信息，补足全局依赖与跨patch信息。3) 提出基于累积条件熵的动态Token过滤（DTF），按区域信息量自适应保留/丢弃token，实现不均匀分配与压缩。

Result: 在实验中取得SOTA：gFID提升约1.3倍（更低更好）且推理提速约8.7倍；在同等或更少token数下维持/提升重建质量，长序列处理更高效。

Conclusion: 基于信息熵的自适应token分配和全局互信息建模有效缓解信息不足与冗余问题，实现更压缩但更准确的图像tokenization，为长序列视觉建模提供可扩展方向。

Abstract: Accurate and effective discrete image tokenization is crucial for long image sequence processing. However, current methods rigidly compress all content at a fixed rate, ignoring the variable information density of images and leading to either redundancy or information loss. Inspired by information entropy, we propose TaTok, a Theoretically grounded adaptive image Tokenization framework. We rigorously identify two key drawbacks in existing methods: information insufficiency when reconstructing images with patch tokens alone, and information redundancy among patch tokens. To address these, we introduce global tokens that model mutual information across patch tokens, and a Dynamic Token Filtering (DTF) algorithm based on cumulative conditional entropy to eliminate redundancy. Experiments confirm TaTok's state-of-the-art performance, delivering a 1.3x gFID improvement and 8.7x inference speedup. By allocating tokens according to information richness, TaTok enables more compressed yet accurate image tokenization, offering valuable insights for future research.

</details>


### [11] [Hilbert-Geo: Solving Solid Geometric Problems by Neural-Symbolic Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16385)
*Ruoran Xu,Haoyu Cheng,Bin Dong,Qiufeng Wang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出Hilbert-Geo统一形式语言与Parse2Reason两步法，把三维立体几何题转为形式化谓词与定理库推理，实现可验证的人类可读解题，在自建SolidFGeo2k/PlaneFGeo3k与MathVerse-Solid上达SOTA。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有多模态几何推理多聚焦于平面几何，面对含三维图的立体几何因空间关系复杂与推理链长而性能低；缺少统一可计算的形式语言与可复用定理库，难以产生可验证的严谨推理过程。

Method: 1) 构建Hilbert-Geo统一形式语言框架：谓词库+定理库；2) Parse2Reason两步法：Parsing—用条件描述语言CDL把自然语言题干与立体几何图同时解析为形式化谓词；Reasoning—基于CDL表示与定理库进行关系推理与代数计算，生成严格可检验且可读的证明/解题过程；框架亦适用于平面几何。并发布两个人工标注数据集SolidFGeo2k与PlaneFGeo3k（含形式标注、解与答案）。

Result: 在SolidFGeo2k上77.3%准确率、MathVerse-Solid上84.1%，显著优于Gemini-2.5-pro(54.2%)与GPT-5(62.9%)；在PlaneFGeo3k上80.2%，显示框架通用性。

Conclusion: 统一的形式语言+两步解析-推理范式能有效解决立体与平面几何多模态推理，生成可验证解题并大幅超越主流MLLMs；代码与数据将开源，推动几何推理研究。

Abstract: Geometric problem solving, as a typical multimodal reasoning problem, has attracted much attention and made great progress recently, however most of works focus on plane geometry while usually fail in solid geometry due to 3D spatial diagrams and complex reasoning. To bridge this gap, we introduce Hilbert-Geo, the first unified formal language framework for solid geometry, including an extensive predicate library and a dedicated theorem bank. Based on this framework, we propose a Parse2Reason method containing two steps of first parsing then reasoning. In the parsing step, we utilize conditional description language (CDL), a formalized language composed of predicates specifically designed to construct geometric conditions, to represent both problem description (natural text) and solid diagrams (visual image). In the reasoning step, we leverage those formal CDL and the theorem bank to perform relational inference and algebraic computation, generating strictly correct, verifiable, and human-readable reasoning processes. Notably, our proposed Hilbert-Geo is also applicable to plane geometry. To advance geometric reasoning, we curate two expert-annotated dataset SolidFGeo2k and PlaneFGeo3k, which are furnished with geometric formal language annotations, solutions and answers. Extensive experiments show that our proposed method achieves the state-of-the-art (SOTA) performance 77.3% in SolidFGeo2k and 84.1% in MathVerse-Solid (one small subset in MathVerse dedicated to solid geometry), substantially outperforming leading MLLMs, such as Gemini-2.5-pro (54.2% on SolidFGeo2k) and GPT-5 (62.9% on MathVerse-Solid). In addition, our method achieves the SOTA accuracy 80.2% in PlaneFGeo3k, demonstrating the generality of the Hilbert-Geo in geometric reasoning. Our code and datasets will be publicly available.

### [12] [Auditing Multimodal LLM Raters: Central Tendency Bias in Clinical Ordinal Scoring](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16386)
*Jiaqing Zhang,Sandeep Elluri,Bhanu Cherukuvada,Yonah Joffe,Jessica Sena,Miguel Contreras,Scott Siegel,Subhash Nerella,Catherine Price,Parisa Rashidi*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文评估多模态大模型在临床时钟绘图测试（CDT）打分中的表现，发现其总体容错一致性尚可，但存在显著“向中间收缩”的打分偏差，尤其损害临床关键的极端分数；最佳校准来自全量微调的视觉Transformer，建议在高风险场景前进行校准感知评估与后验校准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM正被尝试作为临床自动评分员，但其在有序量表（如CDT的Shulman评分）上的打分机制与偏差尚不清楚；需要系统比较LLM与传统监督模型，评估其可用性与风险。

Method: 在两个公开CDT图像数据集上，用Shulman量表打分：比较三类前沿多模态LLM（含零样本与少样本设定）与全量微调的视觉Transformer等监督学习模型；报告MAE与“容错一致性”（如±1分内准确率），并进行逐分值误差与偏差分析；做消融（覆盖全分值少样本、移除临床术语）以探究偏差成因。

Result: 全量微调ViT拥有最佳校准（MAE 0.52，±1分准确率91%）；零样本LLM在容错一致性上具竞争力（例如GPT-5 MAE 0.67，±1分准确率92%），但绝对误差更高。三类LLM均出现显著“中倾偏差/端点压缩”：低分段过预测（0→1），高分段低估（5→4），对临床关键极端分尤为不利；少样本覆盖全分值与去临床术语的提示均无法消除此偏差。

Conclusion: LLM作为评委的偏差从NLP评价延展到临床量表评分：在高风险筛查中应采用校准感知评估，并在部署前进行后验校准或专门校准策略；单靠提示工程与少样本并不能解决端点压缩偏差。

Abstract: Multimodal large language models (LLMs) are increasingly explored as automated evaluators in clinical settings, yet their scoring behavior on ordinal clinical scales remains poorly understood. We benchmark three frontier LLM families against supervised deep learning models for scoring Clock Drawing Test (CDT) images on two public datasets using the Shulman rubric. While fully fine-tuned Vision Transformers achieve the best calibration (MAE 0.52, within-1 accuracy 91%), zero-shot LLMs remain competitive on tolerance-based agreement (GPT-5 MAE 0.67, within-1 accuracy 92%) despite higher absolute error. However, per-score analysis reveals that all three LLM families exhibit a pronounced central tendency effect (systematic endpoint compression): predictions are systematically compressed toward the middle of the scale, with over-prediction at the low end (score 0 to 1) and under-prediction at the high end (score 5 to 4). This effect disproportionately affects the clinically critical extremes where accurate scoring most impacts screening decisions for cognitive impairment. Targeted ablations show that neither few-shot exemplars spanning the full score range nor removing clinical terminology from the prompt eliminates the effect. Our findings extend the LLM-as-a-judge bias literature from NLP evaluation to clinical assessment, and highlight the need for calibration-aware evaluation and post-hoc calibration before deploying LLM-based raters in high-stakes screening workflows.

### [13] [Stabilizing Temporal Inference Dynamics for Online Surgical Phase Recognition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16387)
*Yang Liu,Ning Zhu,Jingjing Peng,Xiwu Chen,Alejandro Granados,Guotai Wang,Sebastien Ourselin*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 作者提出一个统一的“训练-推理-评估”框架来稳定在线外科手术阶段识别的时间一致性，在多个数据集与骨干上显著降低碎片化并保持或略升帧级准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然在线SPR帧级准确率高，但时间维度上不稳定：早期误判会污染时序状态并形成误差级联；真实阶段转换遵循证据累积，而现有多数方法作“无记忆”逐帧判定，易被瞬时置信波动触发错误切换，削弱工作流理解与下游助理可靠性。

Method: 提出模型无关、可插拔的三部分框架：1）训练：Temporal Error-Cascade (TEC)损失，抑制误差起始并稳定时序特征，缓解前向误差传播；2）推理：Evidence-Gated Transition Predictor (EGTP)，基于证据累积设定置信边界，仅在累积证据超过门限时允许阶段跃迁；3）评估：Temporal Fragmentation Index (TFI)，刻画由不稳定引起的时间分裂程度，补充传统帧级/片段度量。

Result: 在Cholec80与AutoLaparo上，跨三种代表性骨干网络，框架显著提升时间稳定性、减少预测碎片化，同时保持或小幅提升帧级性能。

Conclusion: 时间不稳定源于误差级联与转换的证据累积特性。通过TEC稳定特征演化、EGTP在推理时门控转换、TFI衡量碎片化，可在不依赖特定架构的情况下显著提升在线SPR的时序可靠性。

Abstract: Online Surgical Phase Recognition (SPR) models can reach high frame-wise accuracy, yet their predictions often lack temporal stability, fragmenting workflow understanding and reducing the reliability of downstream assistance. We show that this instability is not random noise but arises from two mechanisms: early misclassifications corrupt temporal feature states and propagate forward to form error cascades, and phase transitions follow evidence-accumulation dynamics whereas most online SPR systems rely on memoryless frame-wise decisions, making them sensitive to transient confidence fluctuations. We propose a unified Train-Inference-Evaluation framework that explicitly stabilizes temporal inference dynamics using model-agnostic, plug-and-play components. For training, the Temporal Error-Cascade (TEC) loss suppresses error onset and mitigates forward error propagation by stabilizing temporal feature evolution. For inference, the Evidence-Gated Transition Predictor (EGTP) enforces evidence-driven state transitions, allowing phase changes only when accumulated evidence exceeds a confidence boundary. For evaluation, we introduce the Temporal Fragmentation Index (TFI), a reliability-aware metric that quantifies instability-induced temporal disagreement beyond conventional frame-wise and token-based measures. Experiments on Cholec80 and AutoLaparo across three representative backbones show that the proposed framework substantially improves temporal stability and reduces prediction fragmentation, while maintaining or modestly improving frame-wise performance.

</details>


### [14] [ChronoSC: Task-Oriented Semantic Communication via Temporal-to-Color Encoding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16388)
*Phuc H. Nguyen,Trung T. Nguyen,Quy N. Duong,Van-Dinh Nguyen*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出ChronoSC：把视频时间信息无损压缩到单张“时间-颜色堆叠”图像，并用轻量DeepJSCC端到端传输与重建，结合预训练BLIP做VideoQA，在CLEVRER上以极低带宽保持高精度，最高节省带宽约192倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1) 设计Chrono-Color Stacking：将视频的时序动态编码进一张静态“chrono-image”，号称轻量且无损的时间到颜色投影，实现极致时间压缩；2) 使用轻量DeepJSCC收发器在物理信道上传输并在接收端显式重建该图像；3) 显式重建后直接复用预训练视觉语言模型（BLIP）进行问答推理，对抗噪声与信道失真；4) 端到端管线优化于任务目标（VideoQA）。

Result: 在CLEVRER数据集上，相比原始视频传输，带宽消耗最高减少约192倍，同时保持较高的VideoQA准确率；重建后的chrono-image在噪声条件下仍能被BLIP有效利用。

Conclusion: ChronoSC通过“时间压到图像”的显式表达+DeepJSCC传输，实现任务导向的极致视频时序压缩，在低资源场景下以低带宽和低时延支持VideoQA，并能无缝复用现有大规模预训练视觉语言模型。

Abstract: Semantic communication (SC) aims to reduce transmission overhead by conveying task-relevant information rather than raw data. However, existing SC approaches for video largely focus on pixel-level reconstruction or rely on complex spatiotemporal pipelines, leading to excessive bandwidth usage and latency that are unsuitable for low-resource deployments. In this paper, we propose ChronoSC, a task-oriented semantic communication framework for Video Question Answering (VideoQA). ChronoSC introduces Chrono-Color Stacking, a lightweight and lossless projection scheme that encodes temporal video dynamics into a single static image, enabling extreme temporal compression before transmission. This compact semantic representation is transmitted using a lightweight Deep Joint Source-Channel Coding (DeepJSCC) transceiver and explicitly reconstructed at the receiver. Unlike latent-space methods, explicit visual reconstruction enables the direct reuse of pre-trained vision-language models; specifically, a pre-trained BLIP model is employed to infer answers from noisy, reconstructed chrono-images. Experiments on the CLEVRER dataset show that ChronoSC achieves up to 192 times bandwidth reduction compared to raw video transmission while maintaining high VideoQA accuracy.

### [15] [Inducing Spatial Locality in Vision Transformers through the Training Protocol](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16390)
*Eduardo Santiago Toledo,Asael Fabian Martínez*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 研究比较两种训练协议对从零训练的ViT早期层注意力“局部性”的影响：现代数据增强（AutoAugment/ColorJitter、CutMix、Label Smoothing）显著促使早层注意力更局部、更集中特别是CutMix起决定作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ViT常被指早期层缺乏卷积式的空间局部性；若无大规模预训练，是否能仅靠训练协议诱导局部性尚不清楚。作者希望找出能否以及通过什么机制在早层形成局部注意力。

Method: 固定ViT架构与优化器，对比Baseline与现代训练协议，在CIFAR-10/100与Tiny-ImageNet上训练。从注意头层面用平均注意距离（MAD）与归一化熵度量注意力的“局部性与集中度”。并在CIFAR-100上做消融：分别加入/移除AutoAugment、CutMix、Label Smoothing，观察MAD变化以定位致因。

Result: 现代协议在三数据集上均使早期层注意更局部且更集中；如在CIFAR-100上最小MAD由0.316降至0.008。消融显示CutMix是关键：含CutMix条件MAD≈0.024；不含CutMix条件MAD≈0.210。AutoAugment与Label Smoothing对局部性无独立影响。

Conclusion: 通过CutMix引入“从部分区域即可分类”的训练压力，可在无大规模预训练的情况下促使ViT早层自发形成局部注意。建议在小数据集训练ViT时采用CutMix以增强早层局部性。

Abstract: We investigate whether the training protocol can induce spatial locality in the early layers of a Vision Transformer (ViT) trained from scratch, without large-scale pretraining. Keeping the architecture and optimization procedure fixed, we compare a Baseline protocol with a Modern protocol (AutoAugment/ColorJitter, CutMix, and Label Smoothing) on CIFAR-10, CIFAR-100, and Tiny-ImageNet, characterizing each attention head via Mean Attention Distance (MAD) and normalized entropy. Across all three datasets, the Modern protocol produces more local and more concentrated attention in early layers; on CIFAR-100, the minimum MAD drops from 0.316 (Baseline) to 0.008 (Modern). To identify the source of this effect, we conduct an ablation study on CIFAR-100 by adding or removing each component individually. The results identify CutMix as the determining component within our experiments: all conditions with CutMix exhibit MAD 0.024, while all conditions without CutMix remain at MAD 0.210. AutoAugment and Label Smoothing show no independent effect on locality. Taken together, these findings suggest that the pressure to classify from partial image regions, induced by CutMix, can promote the emergence of local attention in Vision Transformers.

### [17] [Beyond MMSE: Enhancing PnP Restoration with ProxiMAP](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16396)
*Kenta Vert,Giacomo Meanti,Scott Pesme,Michael Arbel,Julien Mairal*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出ProxiMAP：在PnP框架中用“与训练噪声匹配的MAP近似”替代直接MAP或MMSE，避免收敛到卡通化结果，并在多种逆问题上带来更锐利重建。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: PnP常用MMSE去噪器替代难以求解的MAP，但出现“目标-工具不匹配”。近期尝试用扩散分数逼近MAP，但实测学习到的分数与真实分数偏差导致收敛解不真实（卡通化），反而需提前停止。作者希望既利用MAP目标，又避免分数失配导致的收敛失败。

Method: 基于“保持迭代残余噪声与去噪器训练噪声匹配”的原则，设计ProxiMAP：通过噪声调度在迭代过程中维持分布内输入，使得分数估计可靠，形成隐式早停；作为模块化替换，可直接插入标准PnP算法中。另提出混合变体：仅在后期迭代使用ProxiMAP，以更低计算成本达到相当或更好性能。

Result: 直接用学习分数追MAP会收敛到卡通化图像，最佳效果出现在未收敛时。采用ProxiMAP后，重建在去模糊、修补、超分与相位恢复等任务中更锐利且稳定；混合变体在保持或提升质量的同时显著降低计算量。

Conclusion: 面向MAP的迭代若不考虑分数失配会出现收敛失败；通过与训练噪声匹配的近似（ProxiMAP）可让去噪器处于分布内，带来隐式早停与更佳重建，并可作为PnP的通用模块或其低成本混合版本。

Abstract: Plug-and-Play (PnP) methods have become standard tools for solving imaging inverse problems by replacing the intractable maximum a posteriori (MAP) denoiser with the MMSE one. While this mismatch has been widely treated as unavoidable, recent works have sought to close this gap by targeting the MAP with diffusion-model scores. We show this is problematic in practice: learned scores do not match the true ones, so MAP-targeting iterations converge to cartoon-like images rather than realistic ones, and better results are obtained by stopping short of convergence. We turn this observation into a design principle and introduce ProxiMAP, an iterative MAP approximation whose noise schedule keeps the iterate's residual noise matched to the denoiser's training noise. This keeps the denoiser in-distribution where its score is reliable, and yields implicit early stopping that avoids the failure mode above. ProxiMAP is a modular drop-in replacement for MMSE denoisers in standard PnP algorithms and consistently sharpens reconstructions across deblurring, inpainting, super-resolution, and phase retrieval. Building on the same principle, we propose a hybrid variant that applies ProxiMAP only in the late iterations of PnP, where the denoiser is most reliable -- matching or exceeding the full-replacement variant at a fraction of the cost.

</details>


### [18] [Trajectory-Aware Adaptive Inference in Object Detection Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16397)
*Grigorios Papanikolaou,Ioannis Kontopoulos,Giannis Spiliopoulos,Dimitris Zissis,Konstantinos Tserpes*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在YOLOv8检测器上引入早退（early-exit）结构，利用GPS轨迹与运动线索（船间距离、距离收敛速率/相对速度）评估帧级场景复杂度：若短距离且高速汇聚则走全模型，否则仅启用部分子网络；按每帧或每秒帧组动态分配计算。

Result: 在保持“令人满意”的检测性能（精度基本不降）的同时，显著缩短推理时间并降低计算成本，实现精度-效率的可调折中，相比始终用全模型更高效。

Conclusion: 基于运动先验的输入自适应推理可在海事导航中有效削减计算负担且不牺牲关键风险场景的检测质量，为多模态实时感知提供了一种可扩展的效率优先范式。

Abstract: The increasing integration of sensors in autonomous maritime navigation has led to large-scale multimodal datasets, raising challenges in achieving efficient real-time perception. In such systems, object detection and trajectory perception of nearby vessels are tightly coupled, particularly in dynamic environments such as maritime navigation. However, the efficiency of object detection models during inference remains an often-overlooked aspect. To this end, we build upon an existing object detection framework by incorporating GPS trajectory data into the inference process to enable input-adaptive computation. Specifically, we introduce an early-exit mechanism in a YOLOv8-based detector that incorporates motion cues - such as inter-vessel distances. Frames of vessels that are separated by short distances, converging with high speed, are processed using the full model, while only a subset of the network's architecture is activated otherwise. The difficulty degree (or scene complexity) of a frame or set of frames per second is evaluated by leveraging inter-object distance and the rate at which the distance between them decreases. Experimental results demonstrate that this strategy maintains satisfactory detection performance while significantly reducing inference time and computational cost, thus enabling a flexible trade-off between accuracy and efficiency compared to full-model inference.

### [19] [Stable and Near-Reversible Diffusion ODE Solvers for Image Editing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16399)
*Barbora Barancikova,Daniil Shmelev,Cristopher Salvi*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文探讨可逆扩散求解器在文本引导图像编辑中的不稳定性，并提出“近可逆”Runge-Kutta结合向量场平滑的方法，在保持背景的同时提高大幅编辑下的稳定性与编辑忠实度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于DDIM的编辑存在反演误差；完全可逆的ODE求解器虽能消除反演误差，但在需要较大语义/视觉改动时会不稳定、质量骤降。需要一种既尽量保持可逆带来的背景保留优势、又在大编辑下数值稳定的反演方法。

Method: 将扩散反演视为常微分方程数值积分问题：从“严格可逆”求解器转向“近可逆”的Runge-Kutta方法，并配合向量场（评分/漂移场）平滑策略，减小步进误差与刚性导致的不稳定；系统比较背景保留（可逆性优势）与提示对齐（编辑幅度）之间的经验权衡。

Result: 近可逆RK + 向量场平滑在大幅编辑时显著提升编辑稳定性与提示对齐，同时在很大程度上保留背景元素，相比严格可逆方案减少质量崩塌与伪影。

Conclusion: 完全可逆并非最佳：在扩散编辑反演中，选择近可逆且数值稳定的RK求解器并对向量场进行平滑，可在背景保留与提示对齐之间取得更优折衷，实现更高保真、可扩展的编辑。

Abstract: The inversion of diffusion models plays a central role in image editing. Algebraically reversible ODE solvers provide an appealing approach to diffusion inversion for text-guided image editing, by eliminating the inversion error inherent in DDIM-based editing pipelines. However, empirical results indicate that reversibility alone is insufficient. As edits require larger semantic or visual changes, reversible diffusion solvers often exhibit instabilities and suffer sharp drops in output quality. In this paper, we show that the trade-off between exact reversibility and numerical stability manifests empirically as a trade-off between background preservation and prompt alignment in image editing. We then investigate the use of near-reversible Runge-Kutta methods as a more stable alternative to exactly reversible diffusion schemes. When combined with a vector-field smoothing strategy, the resulting approach improves edit fidelity, remains stable under large edits, and largely retains the background-preservation benefits of reversible solvers.

CADS provides a mathematically grounded framework for balancing the cost-accuracy dilemma that dynamically routes samples through a model cascade, ranging from lightweight "Scout" models to high-capacity "Oracle" architectures. Validated on two datasets, CADS demonstrated superior efficiency and accuracy at a computational cost that can be up to 12 times lower than heavy-model inference. ### [22] [When Vision Speaks for Sound](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16403)
*Xiaofei Wen,Wenjie Jacky Mo,Xingyu Fu,Rui Cai,Tinghui Zhu,Wendi Li,Yanan Xie,Muhao Chen,Peng Qi*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文指出当前视频型多模态大模型在“听懂”视频方面常被视觉误导，往往凭视觉线索臆测音频内容而不真正核验音轨。作者提出Thud框架（Shift/ Mute/ Swap三类反事实音频干预）诊断该问题，并给出两阶段对齐方法，用少量偏好数据显著提升音频核验能力，同时保持常规视频/视听问答性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管视频型MLLM发展迅速，但模型在声学理解上出现“视觉牵引”的伪能力：依赖视觉—声学相关性而不检验音视对齐，导致在实际不一致或被篡改音频时仍给出自信但错误的答案。需要一个系统化方法去揭示并缓解这种“音视版Clever Hans”效应。

Method: 1) 提出Thud诊断框架：对同一视频进行三类反事实音频编辑——Shift（时间偏移，测同步）、Mute（静音，测声音是否存在）、Swap（替换，测跨模态一致性），观察模型响应变化以判定是否真正使用音频。2) 训练对齐配方：第一阶段利用干预生成的偏好对（更偏好正确核验音频的回答）进行偏好优化，教会模型做音频核验；第二阶段用事件层面的通用视频偏好数据做正则，避免模型过度专化。

Result: 基于约1万样本的两阶段对齐，模型在三类干预维度上的平均性能提升28个百分点，同时在通用视频与视听问答基准上小幅提升，未出现明显副作用。

Conclusion: 现有视频MLLM普遍存在“以视觉代音”的Clever Hans失效模式。Thud能有效诊断该问题，并通过小规模、针对性的偏好对齐显著增强音频核验与音视一致性能力，且不牺牲通用任务表现。

Abstract: Despite rapid progress in video-capable MLLMs, we find that their apparent audio understanding in videos is often vision-driven: models rely on visual cues to infer or hallucinate acoustic information, rather than verifying the audio stream. This issue appears across both state-of-the-art open-source omni models and leading closed-source models from providers such as Google and OpenAI. We characterize this failure mode as an audio-visual Clever Hans effect, in which models appear (falsely) audio-grounded, but actually exploit visual-acoustic correlations without verifying whether the audio and visual streams are truly aligned. To systematically study this behavior, we introduce Thud, an intervention-driven probing framework based on three counterfactual audio edits: Shift, which tests temporal synchronization; Mute, which tests sound existence; and Swap, which tests audio-visual consistency. Beyond diagnosis, we further study a two-stage alignment recipe: intervention-derived preference pairs teach audio verification, while event-level general video preferences regularize the model against over-specialization. Our best 10K-sample recipe improves average performance across the three intervention dimensions by 28 percentage points, while slightly improving performance on general video and audio-visual QA benchmarks.

### [23] [Hybrid Quantum-MambaVision: A Quantum-enhanced State Space Model for Calibrated Mixed-type Wafer Defect Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16404)

Abstract: Extracting actionable knowledge from industrial visual data is fundamentally bottlenecked by extreme class imbalance and the prohibitive computational complexity of modern foundation models. In semi-conductor manufacturing, identifying multi-label wafer defects is a complex spatial data mining task where overlapping patterns obscure critical root-cause signals. While Vision Transformers (ViTs) excel at global dependency extraction, their quadratic scaling renders them inefficient for high-throughput, real-time anomaly detection. To overcome these computational barriers, this paper introduces Hybrid Quantum-MambaVision, a highly efficient architecture tailored for spatial knowledge discovery. We integrate a linear-complexity State-Space Model (SSM) backbone with a Parameterized Quantum Context Adapter (QCA) and Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA). The Mamba backbone efficiently captures long-range spatial dependencies, while the quantum adapter maps compressed latent features into a high-dimensional Hilbert space to disentangle complex, overlapping signatures. On the highly imbalanced MixedWM38 dataset, Hybrid Quantum-MambaVision achieves exceptional multi-label classification performance, significantly reducing the error rate on complex multi-defect topologies compared to classical baselines. The quantum regularizer acts as a profound uncertainty calibrator, substantially reducing Maximum Calibration Error (MCE) and minimizing expected false-positive costs. This work establishes a scalable Quantum-Classical hybrid paradigm for efficient representation learning in industrial data mining.

### [24] [Concepts Worth Having: Refining VLM-Guided Concept Bottleneck Models with Minimal Annotations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16405)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: CBM需要概念级标注以保证可解释性，但真实应用中这类标注稀缺。用VLM自动生成概念虽可扩展，却引入噪声、降低概念质量与可解释性。需要一种在极少人工成本下兼顾可扩展性与高质量概念的方案。

Method: 提出Vision-plus-Human-guided CBM（VH-CBM）：在VLM的嵌入空间中建立高斯过程（GP），利用VLM提供的全局分布信息并将专家对少量样本的密集概念标注进行监督传播，从而为任意目标样本预测更准确且校准良好的概念；并可与主动学习结合以高效选择标注样本。

Result: 在实证评估中，VH-CBM相较仅由VLM引导的CBM，显著提升概念预测准确率；即使只标注约1%的数据也能取得更优表现，同时概念校准更好，并展示了与主动学习的兼容性与收益。

Conclusion: 混合VLM与少量人工标注，通过VLM嵌入空间的GP传播监督，可在极低标注成本下构建更可解释、概念更准确且更好校准的CBM，并可进一步通过主动学习提升效率。

Abstract: Concept-bottleneck models (CBMs) are neural classifiers that compute predictions from high-level concepts extracted from the input. CBMs ensure stakeholders can understand the concepts -- and the predictions they entail -- by learning these from concept-level annotations, which are however seldom available. Recent CBM architectures work around this issue by obtaining annotations from Vision-Language Models (VLMs). While greatly broadening applicability, doing so can yield lower quality concepts and therefore less interpretable models. We strike for a middle ground by introducing Vision-plus-Human-guided CBM (VH-CBM), a hybrid approach that exploits both VLMs and a small amount of dense annotations. VH-CBM employs a Gaussian Process in the VLM's embedding space, which captures useful global information about the target domain, to propagate the expert's supervision to any target data point. Our empirical evaluation shows how VH-CBM predicts more accurate concepts than VLM-guided CBMs even when annotating as little as 1% of the data, while sporting better concept calibration and supporting active learning.

</details>


### [25] [Contrastive-SDXL: Annotation-Preserving Night-Time Augmentation for Pedestrian Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16406)
*Franky George,Muhammad Khalid,Adil Khan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出Contrastive-SDXL：基于SDXL-Turbo并用LoRA微调的昼夜风格迁移与数据增强框架，用于改进夜间行人检测；通过DINOv2引导的补丁级对比损失与多层自注意力一致性、以及对象一致性损失，保留行人与局部语义结构；合成夜景逼真（FID 22.5）；用其合成数据训练的检测器较仅日间数据基线漏检率下降6–7%，接近真实夜间数据训练效果。

Method: 构建Contrastive-SDXL日转夜增强管线：以SDXL-Turbo为生成骨干，采用LoRA微调；引入由预训练DINOv2编码器（而非生成器自身特征）引导的补丁级语义对比损失，结合DINOv2多层自注意力图以同时约束局部与全局语义一致性；加入对象一致性损失，显式鼓励行人保留。用该模型将日间图像翻译为夜间，作为训练数据增强。

Result: 生成质量：FID=22.5，夜景逼真度较高；检测性能：使用合成夜景增强训练，较仅日间数据基线漏检率降低6–7%，性能接近使用真实夜间数据训练的检测器。

Conclusion: 以一致性驱动的扩散模型增强可有效支撑安全关键的夜间行人检测：在保持目标与语义结构的前提下，实现逼真的昼夜翻译，并显著提升检测器夜间性能，缩小与真实夜间数据训练的差距。

Abstract: Night-time pedestrian detection remains challenging because labelled night-time data are limited and large illumination differences make daytime-only trained detectors unreliable. Latent diffusion models (LDMs) provide a powerful basis for image-to-image translation and cross-domain augmentation, but their effectiveness in safety-critical perception depends on whether detector-relevant objects and local semantic structure are preserved when translating between source and target domains. In this work, we present Contrastive-SDXL, a day-to-night augmentation framework for night-time pedestrian detection built on SDXL-Turbo and fine-tuned using Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA). To preserve semantic correspondence between daytime inputs and translated night-time images, we introduce a patch-wise semantic contrastive loss guided by a pretrained DINOv2 encoder rather than generator encoder features. Multi-level DINOv2 self-attention maps enforce both local and global semantic consistency, while an object consistency loss explicitly encourages pedestrian preservation. Contrastive-SDXL produces realistic night-time images, achieving a Frechet Inception Distance (FID) of 22.5. Detectors trained with our synthetic images obtain a 6-7% reduction in miss rate compared with a daytime-only baseline, approaching the performance of detectors trained on real night-time data. These results demonstrate that consistency-driven diffusion augmentation can effectively support safety-critical night-time pedestrian detection.Specific

Method: 训练一个轻量级“提示生成器”模型：给定测试样本，预测应当前置到VLM输入中的“hint”（上下文或步骤性指引），以引导VLM避开其特征性失败模式；整个流程对VLM仅需一次黑盒API调用，不改动权重、无需重复采样。

Our method is motivated by the observation that VLM errors tend to cluster around recurring failure patterns. We therefore train a lightweight hint generator model to predict, for a given test input, which "hint" should be prepended to the prompt, providing targeted contextual or procedural guidance that steers the VLM away from its characteristic failure modes. *Qinwu Xu*

Main category: cs.CV

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 在开源基准与真实多模态评测中，模型更一致地与图像对齐，幻觉率降低，回答更具可解释与信息性；跨模型的质性对比显示在含糊空间与假前提场景优于多款前沿闭源VLM。

Abstract: Hallucination remains a fundamental challenge in vision-language models (VLMs), where autoregressive generation may produce linguistically plausible yet physically inconsistent or visually ungrounded responses due to likelihood maximization under joint probabilistic modeling.
  We propose a stage-wise preference optimization framework for hallucination reduction through targeted multimodal data construction. Rather than directly optimizing on generic instruction-following data, our approach progressively constructs hallucination-focused preference pairs near known failure boundaries. The framework emphasizes ambiguous spatial orientation, object relationships, OCR uncertainty, and adversarial false-premise training. Hallucinated negatives are generated through minimally perturbed yet visually inconsistent alternatives, enabling Direct Preference Optimization (DPO) to better separate grounded reasoning from plausible hallucination.
  Experiments on open-source benchmarks and real-world multimodal evaluation scenarios demonstrate improved grounding consistency, reduced hallucination, and more informative grounded responses. Cross-model qualitative evaluation further shows that the proposed multimodal LLM DPO framework produces more visually grounded responses than several frontier proprietary VLMs, such as in ambiguous spatial reasoning and adversarial false-premise settings. The results suggest that hallucination may arise not only from limited model capacity, but also from inherent tendencies of autoregressive probabilistic generation to favor linguistically plausible continuations under weak visual grounding. Future work may explore physical consistency modeling, uncertainty-aware multimodal reasoning, and architectural alternatives beyond standard autoregressive decoding.

Abstract: We present NERVE (Neuromorphic Vision and Radar Ensemble), a multi-sensor dataset comprising 257 minutes of synchronized recordings from five sensors: two Dynamic Vision Sensors (DVS), an RGB-D camera, and two Radar units (24GHz and 77GHz). Captured across 12 measurement days in office environments, NERVE contains around 600GB of uncompressed temporally aligned data with around 914,000 frames and around 9.6 million RGB COCO-formatted annotations covering 16 relevant object categories. ### [31] [Diffusion Models, Denoiser Architecture and Creativity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16415)
*Itamar Levine,Yair Weiss*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文探讨扩散模型“创造性”（能生成与训练数据不同但真实度高的图像）的来源，指出其根本来自去噪器架构与目标分布的相互作用，而非仅由最优贝叶斯去噪器决定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有结论表明：若去噪器是针对训练集的贝叶斯最优器，扩散模型会复现训练样本，似与实际的“创造性”现象相矛盾。作者为解释这一矛盾，研究不同去噪器架构如何影响生成分布，从而导致创造性或失真。

Method: 理论上：推导生成样本分布关于目标分布与去噪器架构的显式形式，覆盖三类去噪器——线性、多项式、瓶颈。实验上：对常用UNet去噪器做微小架构改动，比较生成图像的创造性形态与逼真度。

Result: 理论：不同架构诱导不同的生成分布；架构偏置与目标分布的耦合决定是否偏离训练数据、偏离到何种形态。实验：微小UNet修改即可显著改变“创造性”，且常导致强烈不真实样本。

Conclusion: 扩散模型的成功依赖于去噪器架构的归纳偏置与真实目标分布的强对齐；创造性并非自动出现，失配会引发非真实的“伪创造性”。

Abstract: The creativity of diffusion models refers to their ability to generate highly realistic images that are different from their training data. Creativity is somewhat surprising since it is known that if the denoiser used in the diffusion model is the Bayes optimal denoiser for a given training set, then the model will simply copy the training samples. In this paper we present empirical and theoretical results that suggest that creativity in diffusion models is due to an interaction between the denoiser architecture and the target distribution. Theoretically, we give explicit forms for the distribution of generated samples as a function of the target distribution and the denoiser architecture for three different denoiser architectures (linear, polynomial, bottleneck). Empirically, we show that small changes in the popular UNET denoiser architecture leads to very different forms of creativity, and these small changes often yield samples that are highly nonrealistic. Taken together, our results show that diffusion models will only be successful if the inductive bias of the denoiser architecture is in strong alignment with the true target distribution.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视觉-语言模型在一般多模态推理上表现强，但面对需要跨区域、非局部、语义易混淆信息整合的场景时，难以在不充分线索下形成可靠推断，即“碎片化视觉推理”问题；缺乏能监督中间推理步骤、对证据贡献进行细粒度评估与优化的机制。

Method: 提出CAVE（基于GRPO的结构化过程奖励）：在交替的视觉-语言推理中，对每一步动作的贡献进行信用分配，利用三类互补过程信号——信念更新（Belief Update）、证据获取（Evidence Acquisition）、自适应聚焦控制（Adaptive Focus Control）——来评估和引导策略学习；同时构建TRACER-Bench，覆盖四种非局部、易混淆推理维度，并提供关键中间证据以监督推理路径。

Result: 在需要整合碎片化视觉证据的公共基准与新提出的TRACER-Bench上取得显著提升；对更长距离与更深层跨区域依赖更稳健；在通用多模态评测上维持具竞争力的表现。

Conclusion: 过程级信用分配与结构化奖励能有效增强VLM的非局部证据整合与稳健的视觉推理能力；TRACER-Bench为此类任务提供了评测与中间监督。

Abstract: Vision-Language Models (VLMs) have achieved strong performance on general multimodal reasoning, yet remain challenged in integrating nonlocal visual information to support semantically underdetermined visual reasoning. We describe this challenge as Fragmented Visual Reasoning. To this end, we propose Credit Assignment for Visual Evidence (CAVE), a structured process-reward method based on GRPO for interleaved visual reasoning. Specifically, CAVE evaluates the contribution of intermediate steps at the action level via three complementary reasoning process signals: belief update, evidence acquisition, and adaptive focus control, thereby guiding the model to optimize each reasoning action and learn more reliable visual reasoning strategies. Meanwhile, we construct TRACER-Bench, which covers four nonlocal and semantically confusable reasoning dimensions and provides key intermediate evidence to supervise reasoning paths. Experiments demonstrate that CAVE substantially improves performance on tasks requiring fragmented visual evidence integration, covering both public benchmarks and our newly introduced TRACER-Bench, while retaining competitive performance on general multimodal evaluations. Further analyses reveal that CAVE effectively improves the visual reasoning capacity and exhibits stronger robustness under longer-range and deeper cross-region dependencies.

Specifically, we devise a cognitive-dynamics-based adaptive blurring mechanism that dynamically integrates center-biased and saliency-guided visual cues via cross-modal attention. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有网络量化在速度-精度间权衡明显，且泛化有限；补偿型方法虽高效通用，但补偿能力有限且对离群值敏感，导致精度下降。

Method: 提出NBC：在后训练量化框架中引入非线性补偿。设计BLT：同时对量化输入与量化误差做双极对数映射以压缩离群值；在该变换空间中仅使用一个轻量线性层进行补偿，从而保持计算效率与简单性。

Result: 在多任务、多模型、多种量化方法上进行了广泛实验，显示NBC在准确率、效率、鲁棒性与通用性方面均优于现有方法。

Abstract: Network quantization has emerged as one of the most practical model compression techniques, which significantly reduces a model's memory and compute consumption by mapping floating-point numbers to low-bit representations. However, existing quantization methods typically suffer from the speed-accuracy tradeoff and limited generalization. To address these issues, recent compensation-based methods offer an efficient yet general solution by introducing additional lightweight linear layers into the quantized network. However, the accuracy of these methods suffers from their limited compensation capability and high sensitivity to outliers. In this paper, we propose Nonlinear Bipolar Compensation (NBC), a post-training quantization approach that introduces nonlinear compensation to reduce the effect of outliers. We further design Bipolar Logarithmic Transformation (BLT), which compresses outliers by mapping both the quantized input and the quantization error into a transformed space. A simple linear layer is then applied for compensation in the transformed space, preserving the efficiency of our method. Extensive experiments across various tasks, models, and quantization methods confirm the effectiveness, efficiency, robustness, and generality of our NBC approach.

Method: 在Unity、CAMUS、EchoNet Dynamic三数据集上以U-Net为基线，系统评估29种增强及其两两组合，多个超参设置、重复实验；以Dice与IoU衡量域内与跨域性能，用独立样本t检验评估统计显著性，重点比较几何、强度与伪影类增强策略。

Conclusion: 针对心超分割，应优先采用解剖合理、幅度适中的几何增强，并以水平翻转为核心进行成对组合；避免过强的强度/伪影增强。该经验法则可作为设计增强策略以提升模型跨数据集鲁棒性与可迁移性的实证指南。

Abstract: Deep learning models for echocardiography segmentation often struggle to generalise across institutions, scanners, and patient populations, where collecting large, consistently annotated datasets is infeasible. Data augmentation is widely used to improve the robustness of deep learning models; however, its role in enhancing cross-dataset generalisability in echocardiography remains insufficiently understood. This study presents a large-scale multi-dataset evaluation of 29 data augmentation techniques and their pairwise combinations for 2D left ventricular segmentation using a U-Net trained on Unity, CAMUS, and EchoNet Dynamic datasets. Each augmentation was explored under several hyperparameter settings and assessed through repeated runs using Dice and IoU in both in-domain and cross-dataset scenarios, with statistical significance quantified via independent t-tests. Results show that anatomically plausible geometric transformations, particularly affine, shift-scale-rotate, perspective, and random horizontal flip, substantially improve cross-dataset performance, whereas aggressive intensity- or artefact-based augmentations often degrade generalisability. Pairwise augmentation combinations outperform individual augmentations and show that moderate flip-centric combinations, especially random horizontal flip with affine, yield consistent gains across most transfer scenarios. These findings provide empirically grounded guidance for designing augmentation policies that enhance the robustness and transferability of echocardiography segmentation models.

### [39] [KVCapsule: Efficient Sequential KV Cache Compression for Vision-Language Models with Asymmetric Redundancy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16439)
*Yingbing Huang,Tharun Adithya Srikrishnan,Steven K. Reinhardt,Deming Chen*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出KVCapsule：一种针对视觉token的KV缓存压缩框架，在不改动预训练VLM主干与注意力计算的前提下，通过轻量级压缩/重建组件，将KV缓存压缩约60%，实现最高2× TPS提升与2.4×内存降低，几乎不损精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: VLM在自回归解码中需存储大量KV缓存。视觉token序列更长、特征更密集且具空间结构，使LLM常用的KV压缩方法直接迁移无效，导致显存/内存成为推理瓶颈。需要一种结构感知、专门面向视觉token的KV压缩方案，以在有限内存下高效推理。

Method: 对视觉token注意力与表示行为进行实证分析，识别其与文本token差异；据此设计KVCapsule：在冻结VLM与不改动注意力模块的设定下，插入轻量压缩与重建组件，仅对视觉token的KV进行胶囊式（capsule-like）压缩与还原，实现结构感知的KV缓存压缩；可无缝集成多种VLM。

Result: 在多种VLM与基准上评测，KVCapsule在约60%的压缩率下，KV缓存内存最高减少2.4×，吞吐（TPS）最高提升2×，同时准确率与回答质量几乎无损。

Conclusion: 视觉token具有与文本不同的结构注意特性，需专门的KV缓存压缩。KVCapsule作为无需改动主干与注意力的插件式方法，提供了在受限内存条件下扩展VLM推理的务实路径，并为结构感知的多模态缓存压缩研究奠定基础。

Abstract: Vision-Language Models (VLMs) have emerged as a critical and fast-growing extension of Large Language Models (LLMs) that enable multimodal reasoning through both text and image inputs. Although VLMs enrich the capabilities of language models, they also inherit and amplify key computational bottlenecks: the memory overhead caused by the large key-value (KV) cache during autoregressive decoding. This challenge is particularly severe in VLMs, where images produce longer token sequences and denser feature representations compared to text. Moreover, the spatial and information-rich nature of vision tokens introduces structured attention patterns that make many LLM-oriented KV cache compression techniques ineffective when applied directly to VLMs.
  In this work, we conduct a detailed empirical analysis of the behavior of vision tokens, highlighting the critical differences from purely text-based models. Based on these insights, we propose KVCapsule, a novel KV cache compression framework for vision tokens. KVCapsule keeps the pretrained VLM backbone frozen, requires no modification to the attention computation modules, and can be integrated into existing VLMs through lightweight compression and reconstruction components. We evaluate KVCapsule on multiple VLMs and benchmark tasks, demonstrating up to 2x improvement in TPS and 2.4x reduction in KV cache memory at a 60% compression ratio, with negligible degradation in accuracy or response quality. Our findings offer practical pathways to scale VLM inference under constrained memory budgets and inspire further research into structure-aware cache compression for multimodal models.

*Daniel Brignac,Fengwei Tian,Banafsheh Latibari,Abhijit Mahalanobis,Ravi Tandon*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出“语义平滑”用于SAR ATR对抗防御：用条件几何视角合成的随机多视图替代各向同性噪声做随机平滑，聚合多视图预测，提升干净精度与对FGSM、PGD及SAR特有攻击（OTSA、SMGAA）的鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统随机平滑依赖各向同性噪声，在SAR这类结构化传感领域难以保持目标语义与成像几何，导致鲁棒性与准确率受限；需要一种既能进行随机化又能保留SAR语义与几何约束的方法。

Method: 提出“语义平滑”：训练一个新颖的视角合成模型，依据SAR采集几何条件，生成多种可能的雷达视图（语义保持的几何变换）；对每个生成视图进行分类，并将多视图预测进行聚合（如投票/平均）以得到最终鲁棒分类器，取代对输入加各向同性噪声的做法。

Result: 在标准攻击（FGSM、PGD）与SAR特定攻击（OTSA、SMGAA）下均表现出更高的鲁棒性，同时提升无攻击下的干净分类精度，相比基于噪声的随机平滑取得一致改进。

Conclusion: 在结构化感知领域，用能保持语义与几何的随机视图合成替代各向同性噪声的随机平滑更有效；语义保持的几何变换为对抗防御提供了有前景的替代路径。

Abstract: Deep neural networks are vulnerable to adversarial perturbations, limiting deployment in safety-critical applications such as synthetic aperture radar (SAR) automatic target recognition (ATR). Randomized smoothing improves robustness by averaging predictions over noisy inputs, but isotropic noise often fails to preserve the semantic structure of SAR imagery. We propose semantic smoothing, a defense that replaces noised-based perturbations with structured randomized transformations generated by a novel view synthesis model. For SAR, we condition on acquisition geometry to synthesize multiple plausible radar views. Predictions across generated randomized views are aggregated to form a robust classifier. Experiments show that semantic smoothing improves robustness against standard attacks, such as FGSM and PGD, and SAR-specific attacks, such as OTSA and SMGAA, while also increasing clean classification accuracy. These results demonstrate that randomized smoothing via semantically preserving geometric transformations is a promising alternative to isotropic noise for adversarial defense in structured sensing domains.

Abstract: Accurate intraoperative and postoperative diagnosis of spread through air spaces (STAS) is essential for guiding surgical decisions and postoperative management in lung cancer. We propose a Diffusion Attention Expert Model (DAEM) to detect STAS in frozen sections (FSs) and paraffin sections (PSs). On an internal dataset, DAEM achieves AUCs of 0.8946 for FSs and 0.9112 for PSs. Validation on external multi-center datasets from eight institutions demonstrates strong generalizability and interpretability. *Sheikh Tanvir Ahmed,Md. Tanvir Raihan*

Method: 构建由检测到的对象形成的场景图，沿图中的k跳路径追踪多跳依赖；设计跨节点、边与多跳路径的多层级对比目标，使表示在对象语义变化下保持稳定，同时对空间布局敏感；以MRCL框架进行预训练。

Abstract: Understanding how objects relate to each other in space is fundamental to scene understanding, yet most contrastive pre-training approaches only model pairwise relationships, leaving richer compositional and multi-hop interactions largely unexplored. We introduce Multi-Hop Relational Contrastive Learning (MRCL), a framework that extends spatial contrastive learning to graph-structured scene representations. By tracing k-hop paths through scene graphs built from detected objects, MRCL captures implicit spatial dependencies that go well beyond what direct object pairs can express. We define a multi-level contrastive objective spanning nodes, edges, and multi-hop paths, encouraging embeddings that remain stable across object semantics while staying responsive to spatial layout. On a GQA subset, MRCL produces spatially-aware representations that improve content-based graph retrieval (NDCG@5 = 0.748) and consistently benefit downstream tasks, including spatial relationship recognition and graph-based question answering. Together, these results suggest that multi-hop relational supervision offers substantially richer structural guidance than pairwise-only methods, leading to visual representations that are more robust, compositional, and geometry-aware.

### [43] [Conservative AI for Safety-Sensitive Medical Image Restoration: Residual-Bounded CT-CTA Enhancement for Intracranial Aneurysm-Relevant Signal Recovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16458)
*Weijun Ma*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一种用于颅内CT/CTA的“保守”图像复原框架：通过受控的残差加法限制编辑幅度与范围，在不破坏关键解剖边界的前提下提升图像质量；在OOD与低剂量外部数据上显示稳定、方向性收益与更小修改足迹，但尚未证明临床诊断有效性。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将复原表述为“残差有界”的2.5D框架：以合成退化的CT/CTA训练，模型仅对中心切片添加学习到的残差；通过编辑控制图限制修改的幅度与空间范围。评估包含：动脉瘤相关恢复矩阵、与高斯基线的成对比较、蒙特卡洛稳定性、解剖学定位的有意义编辑分析、以及在外部低剂量CT上的测试。

Abstract: Image restoration models are increasingly applied to degraded medical scans, but in safety-sensitive settings they must improve image quality without uncontrolled modification of clinically important regions. This is especially relevant for intracranial CT and CT angiography (CTA), where small vessels and aneurysm-relevant cues lie near high-contrast anatomical boundaries. We frame medical image restoration as a conservative AI problem and present a residual-bounded 2.5D restoration framework trained on synthetically degraded CT/CTA inputs. The model adds a learned residual to the original center slice through an edit-control map that limits the magnitude and spatial extent of modification. We evaluate the framework using an aneurysm-relevant image-recovery matrix, paired comparison against a Gaussian baseline, Monte Carlo stability testing, anatomical localization of meaningful edits, and external evaluation on low-dose CT. On 50 out-of-distribution CT-CTA cases, the bounded model achieved a mean target gain of 0.0635, a mean PSNR of 37.51 dB, and an iatrogenic-edit rate of 4.0%. On external low-dose CT, the model was directionally beneficial and produced a substantially smaller modification footprint than the baseline. Meaningful edits concentrated in brain and skull regions while unrelated anatomy showed negligible change. These findings provide preliminary computational evidence that residual-bounded restoration is feasible in boundary-sensitive vascular imaging, but they do not establish clinical diagnostic performance and require expert review and prospective validation before clinical use.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出REC-RL强化学习框架：1) 采用think-range-answer流程，将中间“关注/焦点预测”视为内部决策；2) 使用Group Relative Policy Optimization进行策略更新；3) 设计两类轻量奖励：a) 准确性奖励=区间监督（range-based interval）+ 高斯精度引导（Gaussian-based precision）以平衡粗到细的计数与定位；b) 格式奖励，强制结构化输出；无需额外标注。

Conclusion: 通过将中间视觉推理纳入RL优化并以组相对策略优化与轻量奖励约束，REC-RL无需额外标注即可更贴合人类感知，提升REC的准确性、可解释性与泛化性。

Abstract: Referring expression counting (REC) is an intention-driven task that requires context-aware visual reasoning. While recent vision-language models incorporate language for visual understanding, most existing REC methods rely on rulebased reinforcement learning with rewards focused primarily on final accuracy, overlooking the quality of intermediate reasoning. We propose REC-RL, a reinforcement learning framework that introduces a think-range-answer paradigm to explicitly optimize the visual reasoning process. RECRL employs Group Relative Policy Optimization and two lightweight rewards: an accuracy reward that combines range-based interval supervision with Gaussian-based precision guidance, and a format reward that enforces structured outputs. By modeling intermediate focus prediction as internal decision-making, REC-RL avoids additional annotations and better aligns with human perception. Extensive experiments demonstrate consistent improvements over strong baselines and robust generalization across benchmarks.

To address the limitations of CNNs in modeling long-range dependencies, and the heavy computational and memory overhead and inter-block contextual in coherence of Transformers in 3D MRI, this paper proposes Multi-Head Mamba (MHMamba). This method combines a U-shaped architecture with a multi-head state-space model (Mamba), splitting the channel dimension into parallel SSM heads and aggregating them with residuals. This enhances long-range representation and improves the stability of multimodal training while maintaining linear complexity. To further align statistics and enhance lesion response, we designed a channel-space calibration module for multi-head outputs and introduced an adaptive fusion mechanism at skip connections to dynamically connect global semantics with local details, thereby improving boundary consistency and the detection of small-volume lesions. We conducted experiments and ablations on BraTS2021 and BraTS2023. The results showed that MHMamba achieved stable and significant improvements in overall accuracy, boundary smoothness, and sensitivity to tumor core and small-volume enhancement areas, while preserving the linear-complexity advantage of Mamba-based modeling, thus verifying the effectiveness and versatility of the method.

### [46] [Mechanistically Interpretable Neural Encoding Reveals Fine-Grained Functional Selectivity in Human Visual Cortex](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16468)
*Idan Daniel Grosbard,Mor Geva,Galit Yovel*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出MINE框架，将机制可解释性应用于神经编码，定位并语义化描述驱动单体素视觉皮层反应的图像特征，并以生成与反事实编辑实验提供因果验证。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出Mechanistically Interpretable Neural Encoding（MINE）：1）使用与语言对齐的图像表示预测单体素反应；2）对每张图像提取并用语义标签描述对体素激活至关重要的特征；3）将跨图像的重要特征概括为每个体素的功能画像；4）通过图像生成与反事实编辑（插入/移除特征）来验证。

Result: MINE生成的每图像特征可用于合成图像，诱发与原图相当的体素反应，优于随机或低归因对照；插入/移除预测特征使体素激活按预期上/下降；基于体素功能画像指导的反事实编辑产生更强的激活变化；在经典类别选择性区中，恢复既有类别偏好并揭示区域内细粒度体素差异。

Conclusion: 机制可解释性可用于打开神经编码黑箱，提供细粒度、语义化且可因果验证的体素级选择性假设，为理解人类视觉皮层功能提供新路径。

Abstract: A central goal in understanding human vision is to uncover the visual features that drive neuronal activity. A growing body of work has used artificial neural networks as encoding models to predict cortical responses to natural images, revealing the visual content that activates category-selective regions. However, existing approaches are largely correlational and treat the encoder as a black box, leaving open which image features drive each voxel's response. We introduce Mechanistically Interpretable Neural Encoding (MINE), a framework that opens this black box by applying mechanistic-interpretability tools to localize the features within natural images that drive millimeter-scale (voxel-level) activity. MINE predicts each voxel's response using language-aligned image representations, and produces semantically interpretable descriptions of the features critical for the voxel's activation. We further generalize these per-image features into per-voxel functional profiles. To validate the per-image descriptions, we show they are sufficient to generate images that elicit voxel responses matching the responses to the original images, more accurately than images generated from random or low-attribution controls. Moreover, counterfactually inserting or removing the predicted features from images shifts activation in the expected direction, providing causal evidence. Counterfactual editing guided by the per-voxel activation profiles produces even stronger activation shifts, indicating that the profiles faithfully capture each voxel's selectivity. Finally, we apply MINE to well-studied category-selective brain regions, showing it recovers their known categorical preferences while revealing fine-grained unique voxel structure within each region. Overall, our results establish mechanistic interpretability as a path to discover and causally validate fine-grained hypotheses about neural function.

### [47] [Visual Agentic Memory: Enabling Online Long Video Understanding via Online Indexing, Hierarchical Memory, and Agentic Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16481)
*Aiden Yiliu Li,Nels Numan,Anthony Steed*

TL;DR: 提出Visual Agentic Memory（VAM），一个训练-free的长视频记忆与检索框架，通过在线索引、层次化并行记忆与“代理式”检索，实现可检查、可查询的视觉证据持久化与基于证据的推理，在OVO-Bench与MM-Lifelong等基准上优于或接近更大模型端到端方案。

Method: 提出训练-free框架VAM，包括：1）Online Indexing：在流式输入下选择性保留证据并建立索引；2）Hierarchical Memory：以并行表示（Parallel Representation）对齐时间上下文与空间观测，层次化组织记忆；3）Agentic Retrieval：以代理式流程搜索、检查与核验候选证据，再据此生成有依据的答案。

Abstract: Long video understanding requires more than large context windows. It also needs a memory mechanism that decides what visual evidence to retain, keeps it searchable over long horizons, and grounds later reasoning in recoverable observations rather than compressed latent state alone. We propose Visual Agentic Memory (VAM), a training-free framework with three components. Online Indexing supports selective evidence retention under streaming constraints. Hierarchical Memory organises retained evidence in a Parallel Representation that aligns temporal context with spatial observations. Agentic Retrieval searches, inspects, and verifies candidate evidence before producing a grounded answer. On OVO-Bench, VAM achieves the highest RT+BT average (68.41) across all reported baselines, improving over end-to-end use of the same underlying MLLM (Gemini 3 Flash, 67.46). On the month-scale split of MM-Lifelong train@month (105.6 hours over 51 days), VAM reaches 17.11%, second only to ReMA with GPT-5 (17.62%). These results suggest that long-horizon video understanding benefits from treating visual memory as an explicit, inspectable, and queryable substrate. Code is available at https://github.com/yiliu-li/Visual-Agentic-Memory.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 动物伪装常以“与环境无缝融合”描述，但缺乏统一、可重复的定量标准；现有评估与生成方法或依赖主观打分，或目标不匹配（通用扩散损失），或受数据集遮挡偏差影响。

Method: 将评估表述为视觉定位问题：给定图像与目标物种，产生类别条件的候选检测，提取分割掩膜，选取其并集与真值掩膜的IoU最高的子集；分数为1减去该最大可恢复定位信号（越高越难被定位→伪装越强）。用人类2AFC实验验证一致性；再将SeamCam作为DPO偏好信号微调扩散式inpainting伪装生成器；构建CamFG-1.5k无遮挡高分辨率基准集。

Result: SeamCam在人类2AFC的2390对比、94名参与者中与人类判断一致率78.82%，较SOTA提升约25%。用作DPO偏好信号可高效训练伪装生成模型，客观函数与任务对齐。发布1,521张图像的数据集CamFG-1.5k以公平评测。

Conclusion: SeamCam提供了首个面向“已知类别下的不可定位性”的统一量化指标，既能与人类感知强相关，又能直接驱动生成模型优化；配合无遮挡数据集，有望成为伪装评估与生成的新标准。

Abstract: Animals are described as effectively camouflaged when they blend seamlessly with their surrounding, yet no standardized quantitative measure of this seamlessness exists. We address this gap by framing camouflage evaluation as a visual localization problem: a well-camouflaged animal is one that remains difficult to detect even when its category is known. We introduce SeamCam (Seamless Camouflage), a metric that quantifies how detectable an animal is from the available visual evidence. Given an image and a target species, SeamCam generates category-conditioned detection proposals, extracts segmentation masks, and identifies the subset whose collective union yields the highest IoU with the ground-truth mask. The SeamCam score is one minus this maximum recoverable localization signal, where a higher score indicates stronger camouflage (i.e., lower detectability). In a human two-alternative forced-choice study with 94 participants and 2,390 comparisons, SeamCam achieves 78.82% agreement with human camouflage difficulty judgments, outperforming state-of-the-art by about 25%. We then demonstrate SeamCam's utility as a preference signal for Direct Preference Optimization (DPO) to fine-tune a diffusion-based inpainting model for camouflage generation. This offers an affordable training approach with an objective explicitly suited for camouflage generation, unlike typical diffusion models. To support rigorous benchmarking, we further introduce CamFG-1.5k, a curated dataset of 1,521 high-resolution images in which animals are fully visible prior to camouflage generation, enabling unbiased evaluation by controlling for occlusion artifacts present in existing datasets. https://7amin.github.io/SeamCam/

</details>

*Zhuoyu Wu,Wenhui Ou,Lexi Zhang,Pei-Sze Tan,Dongjun Wu,Junhe Zhao,Wenqi Fang,Raphaël C. -W. Phan*
